data_ingestion.py
```python
'''
Module for data ingestion and cleaning.
'''
import pandas as pd
import logging

class DataIngestion:
    def __init__(self):
        logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s')

    def ingest_data(self):
        # Load OBD data and sensor feeds
        try:
            data = pd.read_csv('obd_data.csv')  # Example file path
            logging.info("Data loaded successfully.")
        except FileNotFoundError:
            logging.error("Data file not found. Please check the file path.")
            data = pd.DataFrame()  # Return empty DataFrame if file not found
        except pd.errors.EmptyDataError:
            logging.error("Data file is empty.")
            data = pd.DataFrame()
        except pd.errors.ParserError:
            logging.error("Error parsing data file.")
            data = pd.DataFrame()
        return data

    def clean_data(self, data):
        # Clean and preprocess the data
        if data.empty:
            logging.error("No data to clean. Exiting process.")
            return pd.DataFrame()
        cleaned_data = data.dropna()  # Example cleaning step
        # Additional cleaning steps can be added here
        logging.info("Data cleaned successfully.")
        return cleaned_data

    def label_data(self, cleaned_data):
        # Label the data for training
        if cleaned_data.empty:
            logging.error("No data to label. Exiting process.")
            return pd.DataFrame()
        if 'fault_code' in cleaned_data.columns:
            cleaned_data['label'] = cleaned_data['fault_code'].apply(lambda x: 1 if x else 0)
        else:
            cleaned_data['label'] = 0  # Default label if no fault_code column
        logging.info("Data labeled successfully.")
        return cleaned_data
```

model_training.py
```python
'''
Module for model training and validation.
'''
from sklearn.model_selection import train_test_split
from sklearn.ensemble import RandomForestClassifier
import logging

class ModelTraining:
    def __init__(self):
        logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s')

    def train_model(self, data):
        # Train the model
        if data.empty:
            logging.error("No data available for training. Exiting process.")
            return None
        X = data.drop('label', axis=1)
        y = data['label']
        try:
            X_train, X_test, y_train, y_test = train_test_split(X, y, test_size=0.2)
            model = RandomForestClassifier()
            model.fit(X_train, y_train)
            logging.info("Model trained successfully.")
            return model
        except ValueError as e:
            logging.error(f"Error during model training: {str(e)}")
            return None

    def validate_model(self, model, data):
        # Validate the model's performance
        if model is None or data.empty:
            logging.error("Model validation failed due to lack of data or model.")
            return
        X = data.drop('label', axis=1)
        y = data['label']
        score = model.score(X, y)
        logging.info(f"Model validation score: {score}")
```

main.py
```python
'''
Main file to orchestrate the vehicle diagnostics system.
'''
from data_ingestion import DataIngestion
from model_training import ModelTraining
from api import API
from dashboard import Dashboard

def main():
    # Data ingestion and cleaning
    data_ingestion = DataIngestion()
    raw_data = data_ingestion.ingest_data()
    if raw_data.empty:
        return  # Exit if no data is ingested
    cleaned_data = data_ingestion.clean_data(raw_data)
    if cleaned_data.empty:
        return  # Exit if no data is cleaned
    labeled_data = data_ingestion.label_data(cleaned_data)
    if labeled_data.empty:
        return  # Exit if no data is labeled

    # Model training and validation
    model_training = ModelTraining()
    model = model_training.train_model(labeled_data)
    if model is None:
        return  # Exit if model training failed
    model_training.validate_model(model, labeled_data)

    # API exposure
    api = API()
    api.create_api(model)

    # Dashboard creation
    dashboard = Dashboard()
    dashboard.create_dashboard()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```

model_training.py
```python
'''
Module for model training and validation.
'''
from sklearn.model_selection import train_test_split
from sklearn.ensemble import RandomForestClassifier
import logging

class ModelTraining:
    def __init__(self):
        logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s')

    def train_model(self, data):
        # Train the model
        if data.empty:
            logging.error("No data available for training. Exiting process.")
            return None
        X = data.drop('label', axis=1)
        y = data['label']
        try:
            X_train, X_test, y_train, y_test = train_test_split(X, y, test_size=0.2)
            model = RandomForestClassifier()
            model.fit(X_train, y_train)
            logging.info("Model trained successfully.")
            return model
        except ValueError as e:
            logging.error(f"Error during model training: {str(e)}")
            return None

    def validate_model(self, model, data):
        # Validate the model's performance
        if model is None or data.empty:
            logging.error("Model validation failed due to lack of data or model.")
            return
        X = data.drop('label', axis=1)
        y = data['label']
        score = model.score(X, y)
        logging.info(f"Model validation score: {score}")

Task: "Please help me implement a Python program to develop a bespoke AI model for vehicle diagnostics that ingests, cleans, and labels OBD data and sensor feeds, trains and validates a model for fault detection and anomaly classification, and exposes a documented API with a lightweight dashboard for real-time insights.".

"main.py
```python
'''
Main file to orchestrate the vehicle diagnostics system.
'''
from data_ingestion import DataIngestion
from model_training import ModelTraining
from api import API
from dashboard import Dashboard
def main():
    # Data ingestion and cleaning
    data_ingestion = DataIngestion()
    raw_data = data_ingestion.ingest_data()
    if raw_data.empty:
        return  # Exit if no data is ingested
    cleaned_data = data_ingestion.clean_data(raw_data)
    if cleaned_data.empty:
        return  # Exit if no data is cleaned
    labeled_data = data_ingestion.label_data(cleaned_data)
    if labeled_data.empty:
        return  # Exit if no data is labeled
    # Model training and validation
    model_training = ModelTraining()
    model = model_training.train_model(labeled_data)
    if model is None:
        return  # Exit if model training failed
    model_training.validate_model(model, labeled_data)
    # API exposure
    api = API()
    api.create_api(model)
    # Dashboard creation
    dashboard = Dashboard()
    dashboard.create_dashboard()
if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```

data_ingestion.py
```python
'''
Module for data ingestion and cleaning.
'''
import pandas as pd
import logging
class DataIngestion:
    def __init__(self):
        logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s')
    def ingest_data(self):
        # Load OBD data and sensor feeds
        try:
            data = pd.read_csv('obd_data.csv')  # Example file path
            logging.info("Data loaded successfully.")
        except FileNotFoundError:
            logging.error("Data file not found. Please check the file path.")
            data = pd.DataFrame()  # Return empty DataFrame if file not found
        except pd.errors.EmptyDataError:
            logging.error("Data file is empty.")
            data = pd.DataFrame()
        except pd.errors.ParserError:
            logging.error("Error parsing data file.")
            data = pd.DataFrame()
        return data
    def clean_data(self, data):
        # Clean and preprocess the data
        if data.empty:
            logging.error("No data to clean. Exiting process.")
            return pd.DataFrame()
        cleaned_data = data.dropna()  # Example cleaning step
        # Additional cleaning steps can be added here
        logging.info("Data cleaned successfully.")
        return cleaned_data
    def label_data(self, cleaned_data):
        # Label the data for training
        if cleaned_data.empty:
            logging.error("No data to label. Exiting process.")
            return pd.DataFrame()
        if 'fault_code' in cleaned_data.columns:
            cleaned_data['label'] = cleaned_data['fault_code'].apply(lambda x: 1 if x else 0)
        else:
            cleaned_data['label'] = 0  # Default label if no fault_code column
        logging.info("Data labeled successfully.")
        return cleaned_data
```

model_training.py
```python
'''
Module for model training and validation.
'''
from sklearn.model_selection import train_test_split
from sklearn.ensemble import RandomForestClassifier
import logging
class ModelTraining:
    def __init__(self):
        logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s')
    def train_model(self, data):
        # Train the model
        if data.empty:
            logging.error("No data available for training. Exiting process.")
            return None
        X = data.drop('label', axis=1)
        y = data['label']
        try:
            X_train, X_test, y_train, y_test = train_test_split(X, y, test_size=0.2)
            model = RandomForestClassifier()
            model.fit(X_train, y_train)
            logging.info("Model trained successfully.")
            return model
        except ValueError as e:
            logging.error(f"Error during model training: {str(e)}")
            return None
    def validate_model(self, model, data):
        # Validate the model's performance
        if model is None or data.empty:
            logging.error("Model validation failed due to lack of data or model.")
            return
        X = data.drop('label', axis=1)
        y = data['label']
        score = model.score(X, y)
        logging.info(f"Model validation score: {score}")
```

api.py
```python
'''
Module for API exposure.
'''
from flask import Flask, request, jsonify
class API:
    def create_api(self, model):
        app = Flask(__name__)
        @app.route('/predict', methods=['POST'])
        def predict():
            # Implement logic to accept input data for prediction
            input_data = request.json.get('data', [])
            if not input_data:
                return jsonify({'error': 'No input data provided'}), 400
            try:
                # Validate input data
                if not isinstance(input_data, list) or not all(isinstance(i, (int, float)) for i in input_data):
                    return jsonify({'error': 'Invalid input data format'}), 400
                prediction = model.predict([input_data])
                return jsonify({'prediction': prediction.tolist()})
            except Exception as e:
                return jsonify({'error': str(e)}), 500
        app.run(debug=True)
```

dashboard.py
```python
'''
Module for dashboard creation using tkinter.
'''
import tkinter as tk
import requests
import threading
class Dashboard:
    def create_dashboard(self):
        # Create a simple dashboard using tkinter
        root = tk.Tk()
        root.title("Vehicle Diagnostics Dashboard")
        label = tk.Label(root, text="Real-time Insights")
        label.pack()
        data_label = tk.Label(root, text="Fetching data...")
        data_label.pack()
        def fetch_data():
            try:
                # Example input data provided as a valid Python list
                response = requests.post('http://127.0.0.1:5000/predict', json={'data': [0, 1, 2]})
                if response.status_code == 200:
                    prediction = response.json().get('prediction', 'No data')
                    data_label.config(text=f"Prediction: {prediction}")
                else:
                    data_label.config(text=f"Error: {response.json().get('error', 'Unknown error')}")
            except Exception as e:
                data_label.config(text=f"Error fetching data: {str(e)}")
            # Schedule the next update
            root.after(5000, fetch_data)  # Update every 5 seconds
        # Start fetching data
        threading.Thread(target=fetch_data).start()
        root.mainloop()
```

"main.py
```python
'''
Main file to orchestrate the vehicle diagnostics system.
'''
from data_ingestion import DataIngestion
from model_training import ModelTraining
from api import API
from dashboard import Dashboard
def main():
    # Data ingestion and cleaning
    data_ingestion = DataIngestion()
    raw_data = data_ingestion.ingest_data()
    if raw_data.empty:
        return  # Exit if no data is ingested
    cleaned_data = data_ingestion.clean_data(raw_data)
    if cleaned_data.empty:
        return  # Exit if no data is cleaned
    labeled_data = data_ingestion.label_data(cleaned_data)
    if labeled_data.empty:
        return  # Exit if no data is labeled
    # Model training and validation
    model_training = ModelTraining()
    model = model_training.train_model(labeled_data)
    if model is None:
        return  # Exit if model training failed
    model_training.validate_model(model, labeled_data)
    # API exposure
    api = API()
    api.create_api(model)
    # Dashboard creation
    dashboard = Dashboard()
    dashboard.create_dashboard()
if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

data_ingestion.py
```python
'''
Module for data ingestion and cleaning.
'''
import pandas as pd
import logging
class DataIngestion:
    def __init__(self):
        logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s')
    def ingest_data(self):
        # Load OBD data and sensor feeds
        try:
            data = pd.read_csv('obd_data.csv')  # Example file path
            logging.info("Data loaded successfully.")
        except FileNotFoundError:
            logging.error("Data file not found. Please check the file path.")
            data = pd.DataFrame()  # Return empty DataFrame if file not found
        except pd.errors.EmptyDataError:
            logging.error("Data file is empty.")
            data = pd.DataFrame()
        except pd.errors.ParserError:
            logging.error("Error parsing data file.")
            data = pd.DataFrame()
        return data
    def clean_data(self, data):
        # Clean and preprocess the data
        if data.empty:
            logging.error("No data to clean. Exiting process.")
            return pd.DataFrame()
        cleaned_data = data.dropna()  # Example cleaning step
        # Additional cleaning steps can be added here
        logging.info("Data cleaned successfully.")
        return cleaned_data
    def label_data(self, cleaned_data):
        # Label the data for training
        if cleaned_data.empty:
            logging.error("No data to label. Exiting process.")
            return pd.DataFrame()
        if 'fault_code' in cleaned_data.columns:
            cleaned_data['label'] = cleaned_data['fault_code'].apply(lambda x: 1 if x else 0)
        else:
            cleaned_data['label'] = 0  # Default label if no fault_code column
        logging.info("Data labeled successfully.")
        return cleaned_data
```
model_training.py
```python
'''
Module for model training and validation.
'''
from sklearn.model_selection import train_test_split
from sklearn.ensemble import RandomForestClassifier
import logging
class ModelTraining:
    def __init__(self):
        logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s')
    def train_model(self, data):
        # Train the model
        if data.empty:
            logging.error("No data available for training. Exiting process.")
            return None
        X = data.drop('label', axis=1)
        y = data['label']
        try:
            X_train, X_test, y_train, y_test = train_test_split(X, y, test_size=0.2)
            model = RandomForestClassifier()
            model.fit(X_train, y_train)
            logging.info("Model trained successfully.")
            return model
        except ValueError as e:
            logging.error(f"Error during model training: {str(e)}")
            return None
    def validate_model(self, model, data):
        # Validate the model's performance
        if model is None or data.empty:
            logging.error("Model validation failed due to lack of data or model.")
            return
        X = data.drop('label', axis=1)
        y = data['label']
        score = model.score(X, y)
        logging.info(f"Model validation score: {score}")
```
api.py
```python
'''
Module for API exposure.
'''
from flask import Flask, request, jsonify
class API:
    def create_api(self, model):
        app = Flask(__name__)
        @app.route('/predict', methods=['POST'])
        def predict():
            # Implement logic to accept input data for prediction
            input_data = request.json.get('data', [])
            if not input_data:
                return jsonify({'error': 'No input data provided'}), 400
            try:
                # Validate input data
                if not isinstance(input_data, list) or not all(isinstance(i, (int, float)) for i in input_data):
                    return jsonify({'error': 'Invalid input data format'}), 400
                prediction = model.predict([input_data])
                return jsonify({'prediction': prediction.tolist()})
            except Exception as e:
                return jsonify({'error': str(e)}), 500
        app.run(debug=True)
```
dashboard.py
```python
'''
Module for dashboard creation using tkinter.
'''
import tkinter as tk
import requests
import threading
class Dashboard:
    def create_dashboard(self):
        # Create a simple dashboard using tkinter
        root = tk.Tk()
        root.title("Vehicle Diagnostics Dashboard")
        label = tk.Label(root, text="Real-time Insights")
        label.pack()
        data_label = tk.Label(root, text="Fetching data...")
        data_label.pack()
        def fetch_data():
            try:
                # Example input data provided as a valid Python list
                response = requests.post('http://127.0.0.1:5000/predict', json={'data': [0, 1, 2]})
                if response.status_code == 200:
                    prediction = response.json().get('prediction', 'No data')
                    data_label.config(text=f"Prediction: {prediction}")
                else:
                    data_label.config(text=f"Error: {response.json().get('error', 'Unknown error')}")
            except Exception as e:
                data_label.config(text=f"Error fetching data: {str(e)}")
            # Schedule the next update
            root.after(5000, fetch_data)  # Update every 5 seconds
        # Start fetching data
        threading.Thread(target=fetch_data).start()
        root.mainloop()
```

"main.py
```python
'''
Main file to orchestrate the vehicle diagnostics system.
'''
from data_ingestion import DataIngestion
from model_training import ModelTraining
from api import API
from dashboard import Dashboard
def main():
    # Data ingestion and cleaning
    data_ingestion = DataIngestion()
    raw_data = data_ingestion.ingest_data()
    if raw_data.empty:
        return  # Exit if no data is ingested
    cleaned_data = data_ingestion.clean_data(raw_data)
    if cleaned_data.empty:
        return  # Exit if no data is cleaned
    labeled_data = data_ingestion.label_data(cleaned_data)
    if labeled_data.empty:
        return  # Exit if no data is labeled
    # Model training and validation
    model_training = ModelTraining()
    model = model_training.train_model(labeled_data)
    if model is None:
        return  # Exit if model training failed
    model_training.validate_model(model, labeled_data)
    # API exposure
    api = API()
    api.create_api(model)
    # Dashboard creation
    dashboard = Dashboard()
    dashboard.create_dashboard()
if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```

data_ingestion.py
```python
'''
Module for data ingestion and cleaning.
'''
import pandas as pd
import logging
class DataIngestion:
    def __init__(self):
        logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s')
    def ingest_data(self):
        # Load OBD data and sensor feeds
        try:
            data = pd.read_csv('obd_data.csv')  # Example file path
            logging.info("Data loaded successfully.")
        except FileNotFoundError:
            logging.error("Data file not found. Please check the file path.")
            data = pd.DataFrame()  # Return empty DataFrame if file not found
        except pd.errors.EmptyDataError:
            logging.error("Data file is empty.")
            data = pd.DataFrame()
        except pd.errors.ParserError:
            logging.error("Error parsing data file.")
            data = pd.DataFrame()
        return data
    def clean_data(self, data):
        # Clean and preprocess the data
        if data.empty:
            logging.error("No data to clean. Exiting process.")
            return pd.DataFrame()
        cleaned_data = data.dropna()  # Example cleaning step
        # Additional cleaning steps can be added here
        logging.info("Data cleaned successfully.")
        return cleaned_data
    def label_data(self, cleaned_data):
        # Label the data for training
        if cleaned_data.empty:
            logging.error("No data to label. Exiting process.")
            return pd.DataFrame()
        if 'fault_code' in cleaned_data.columns:
            cleaned_data['label'] = cleaned_data['fault_code'].apply(lambda x: 1 if x else 0)
        else:
            cleaned_data['label'] = 0  # Default label if no fault_code column
        logging.info("Data labeled successfully.")
        return cleaned_data
```

model_training.py
```python
'''
Module for model training and validation.
'''
from sklearn.model_selection import train_test_split
from sklearn.ensemble import RandomForestClassifier
import logging
class ModelTraining:
    def __init__(self):
        logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s')
    def train_model(self, data):
        # Train the model
        if data.empty:
            logging.error("No data available for training. Exiting process.")
            return None
        X = data.drop('label', axis=1)
        y = data['label']
        try:
            X_train, X_test, y_train, y_test = train_test_split(X, y, test_size=0.2)
            model = RandomForestClassifier()
            model.fit(X_train, y_train)
            logging.info("Model trained successfully.")
            return model
        except ValueError as e:
            logging.error(f"Error during model training: {str(e)}")
            return None
    def validate_model(self, model, data):
        # Validate the model's performance
        if model is None or data.empty:
            logging.error("Model validation failed due to lack of data or model.")
            return
        X = data.drop('label', axis=1)
        y = data['label']
        score = model.score(X, y)
        logging.info(f"Model validation score: {score}")
```

api.py
```python
'''
Module for API exposure.
'''
from flask import Flask, request, jsonify
class API:
    def create_api(self, model):
        app = Flask(__name__)
        @app.route('/predict', methods=['POST'])
        def predict():
            # Implement logic to accept input data for prediction
            input_data = request.json.get('data', [])
            if not input_data:
                return jsonify({'error': 'No input data provided'}), 400
            try:
                # Validate input data
                if not isinstance(input_data, list) or not all(isinstance(i, (int, float)) for i in input_data):
                    return jsonify({'error': 'Invalid input data format'}), 400
                prediction = model.predict([input_data])
                return jsonify({'prediction': prediction.tolist()})
            except Exception as e:
                return jsonify({'error': str(e)}), 500
        app.run(debug=True)
```

dashboard.py
```python
'''
Module for dashboard creation using tkinter.
'''
import tkinter as tk
import requests
import threading
class Dashboard:
    def create_dashboard(self):
        # Create a simple dashboard using tkinter
        root = tk.Tk()
        root.title("Vehicle Diagnostics Dashboard")
        label = tk.Label(root, text="Real-time Insights")
        label.pack()
        data_label = tk.Label(root, text="Fetching data...")
        data_label.pack()
        def fetch_data():
            try:
                # Example input data provided as a valid Python list
                response = requests.post('http://127.0.0.1:5000/predict', json={'data': [0, 1, 2]})
                if response.status_code == 200:
                    prediction = response.json().get('prediction', 'No data')
                    data_label.config(text=f"Prediction: {prediction}")
                else:
                    data_label.config(text=f"Error: {response.json().get('error', 'Unknown error')}")
            except Exception as e:
                data_label.config(text=f"Error fetching data: {str(e)}")
            # Schedule the next update
            root.after(5000, fetch_data)  # Update every 5 seconds
        # Start fetching data
        threading.Thread(target=fetch_data).start()
        root.mainloop()
```

# LangChain

Building applications with LLMs through composability

Looking for the JS/TS version? Check out LangChain.js.

**Production Support:** As you move your LangChains into production, we'd love to offer more comprehensive support.

## Quick Install

`pip install langchain`

or

`conda install langchain -c conda-forge`

## 🤔 What is this?

Large language models (LLMs) are emerging as a transformative technology, enabling developers to build applications that they previously could not. However, using these LLMs in isolation is often insufficient for creating a truly powerful app - the real power comes when you can combine them with other sources of computation or knowledge.

This library aims to assist in the development of those types of applications. Common examples of these applications include:

**❓ Question Answering over specific documents**

- Documentation

- End-to-end Example: Question Answering over Notion Database

**🤖 Agents**

- End-to-end Example: GPT+WolframAlpha

```markdown
# Vehicle Diagnostics AI Model

This software is designed to develop a bespoke AI model for vehicle diagnostics. It ingests, cleans, and labels OBD data and sensor feeds, trains and validates a model for fault detection and anomaly classification, and exposes a documented API with a lightweight dashboard for real-time insights.

## Main Functions

1. **Data Ingestion and Cleaning**: 
   - Loads OBD data and sensor feeds.
   - Cleans and preprocesses the data to ensure quality.
   - Labels the data for training purposes.

2. **Model Training and Validation**:
   - Trains a Random Forest Classifier model using the labeled data.
   - Validates the model to ensure its performance and accuracy.

3. **API Exposure**:
   - Exposes a RESTful API using Flask to allow for predictions based on input data.

4. **Dashboard Creation**:
   - Provides a lightweight dashboard using Tkinter for real-time insights and predictions.

## Installation

### Environment Setup

To run this software, you need to have Python installed on your system. You can download Python from [python.org](https://www.python.org/downloads/).

### Install Dependencies

Once Python is installed, you can install the necessary dependencies using pip. Open your terminal or command prompt and run the following command:

```bash
pip install -r requirements.txt
```

This will install the following packages:
- pandas>=1.1.4
- scikit-learn>=0.24.0
- flask>=1.1.2
- requests>=2.24.0

## Usage

### Running the Software

1. **Data Preparation**:
   - Ensure you have your OBD data and sensor feeds available in a CSV format (e.g., `obd_data.csv`).

2. **Start the Application**:
   - Run the main script to start the entire process:
     ```bash
     python main.py
     ```

3. **API Usage**:
   - The API will be exposed at `http://127.0.0.1:5000/predict`.
   - You can send a POST request with JSON data to this endpoint to get predictions. Example:
     ```json
     {
       "data": [0, 1, 2]
     }
     ```

4. **Dashboard**:
   - The dashboard will automatically open and display real-time insights.
   - It fetches data every 5 seconds and updates the display with the latest predictions.

### Troubleshooting

- **Data File Not Found**: Ensure the `obd_data.csv` file is in the correct directory.
- **API Errors**: Check if the Flask server is running and accessible at the specified endpoint.
- **Dashboard Issues**: Ensure Tkinter is properly installed and configured on your system.

## Documentation

For further details and documentation, please refer to the source code comments and logging outputs. The logging provides insights into each step of the process, helping you understand the flow and troubleshoot any issues.

---

This manual provides a comprehensive guide to using the Vehicle Diagnostics AI Model software. For any additional support or inquiries, please contact our support team.
